### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon common name.

### SPARQL:ership.

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene .
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType .
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0000301 .
	?efo_0000301 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism .
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon .
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	FILTER(   ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575   )
	FILTER(   ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType   )
}

19:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value.

### SPARQL:ership.

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX ensembl: <http://rdf.ebi.ac.uk/resource/ensembl/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene .
	?gene lscr:xrefEnsemblGene ensembl:ENSG00000130208 .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage obo:UBERON_0000113 .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 .
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	FILTER(       ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575       )
}

### EXPLANATION:
The query finds the anatomical entity where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage.
The expression level is provided.
The strain is "wild-type".
The gene expression has false discovery rate p-value is provided.

### FILTER:
The anatomical entity should not be an gene.

### ORDER:
The anatomical entity is sorted in ascending order by its label.

### SELECT:
The query returns the anatomical entity label, the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value, the anatomical entity label, the gene expression level, the strain label, the gene.

### DESCRIPTION:
The gene see also list includes the description "an anatomical entity where the gene is expressed".
The expression level is provided.
The strain is "wild-type".
The gene expression has false discovery rate p-value is provided.

21:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also and the gene description.

### SPARQL:
This query has been done using SPARQLquiry. The full query is:

```sparql
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellType ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?expression ?score ?taxon_scientificname ?gene_description ?stage ?gene ?gene_seealso ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene .
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType .
	?cellType rdfs:label "cell type" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage .
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?strain .
	?strain rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism .
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon .
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?strain <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?strain_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(                 ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575                 )
	FILTER(                 ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                 )
}
```

### SPARQL:

	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene .
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType .
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism .
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon .
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(                 ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575                 )
	FILTER(                 ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                 )
}

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the APOC1 gene is expressed? Provide also the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene label.

### SPARQL:ership.

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?gene ?gene_label WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?anatomicalentity .
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity .
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
}

### EXPLANATION:
SPARQL makes it easy to ask for the anatomical entities where a gene is expressed.

In the above example, we ask for the anatomical entity where the gene APOC1 is expressed.

Note that in order to get the anatomical entity label, we use,

    anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label>,

which gives us the anatomical entity label.

Note also that to get the anatomical entity description, we use,

    anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description>,

which gives us the anatomical entity description.

Finally, to get the gene label, we use,

    gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label>,

which gives us the gene label.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?gene ?gene_label WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?anatomicalentity .
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity .
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
}

The brain is protected by the skull. The brain is responsible for the human body's cognitive functions, behavior, emotion, sense of self, and sense of time. It is also responsible for human body movement, speech, and sleep. The brain is the most complex organ in the human body. It is made up of billions of neurons. 37:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the anatomical entity description.

### SPARQL:ership.

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?taxon_scientificname ?stage ?gene WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene .
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType .
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage .
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 .
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism .
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon .
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	FILTER(     ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575     )
	FILTER(     ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType     )
}

### EXPLANATION:
The SPARQL query finds the human gene where the expression level is highest.
The anatomical entity is determined using the expression condition.
The anatomical entity is a cell type, a gene expression is found,
the expression level is calculated.
The expression condition is a post-juvenile stage.
The taxon is human.
The taxon scientific name is provided.
The anatomical entity description is provided.

	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene .

	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .

### INSTRUCTION

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene description.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expression ?score ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_description ?taxon_scientificname ?efo_0005135_label ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?organism ?anatomicalentity_label ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?stage ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?gene_description ?efo_0005135 ?gene ?taxon_commonname WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene .
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType .
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage .
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 .
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism .
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon .
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(                 ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575                 )
	FILTER(                 ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                 )
}

### RESULT:
### http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName?efo_0005135=wild-type&gene=APOC1&expressioncondition=http://purl.org/genex#ExpressionCondition%3Awild-type&expression=http://purl.org/genex#Expression&score=0&anatomicalentity=http://purl.org/genex#AnatomicalEntity%3Acell&anatomicalentityName=cell&cellTypeName=http://purl.org/genex#AnatomicalEntity%3Acell&expression_hase

### SPARQL: opponens_triceps_extensor_sp_0_3.expression.score?expression_level?expression?gene?anatomicalentity?anatomicalentityName?cellType?gene_expression?score?strain?gene_id?expression?expression_score?anatomicalentityName?cellType?gene?gene_id?strain?

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>

	?expression a genex:Expression .

	?cellType rdfs:label "cell type" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?strain .
	?strain rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .

	?gene rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?expression ?gene_expression ?gene .
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_ .
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_score .

	FILTER(   ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType   )
}

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>

	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.

	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType .

	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon .

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also and the gene description.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX ensembl: <http://rdf.ebi.ac.uk/resource/ensembl/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene_description ?gene ?gene_seealso ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene .
	?gene lscr:xrefEnsemblGene ensembl:ENSG00000130208 .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage obo:UBERON_0000113 .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 .
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	FILTER(               ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575               )
}

### RESULT:
    ??? expression ?expression ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?expression ?expression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?gene ?gene_description ?gene_seealso ?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description ?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso ?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description ?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel

69:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the anatomical entity description.

### SPARQL:ampionship.

### ANSWER:
Prepost_juvenile_expression(genei=han_gene,anatomicalentityi=anatomicalentity,anatomicalentityDescriptioni=anatomicalentityDescription,score=expression,efold=3,genef=human)

### EXPLANATION:
The pre-postjuvenile stage is obtained by combining the pre-juvenile stage and the post-juvenile stage. The anatomical entity description is provided by the anatomical entity description. The expression score is provided independently of the strain and the sex. The gene see also is provided by the gene see also. The gene description is provided by the gene description. The gene label is provided by the gene label. The anatomical entity is either the anatomical entity description or the anatomical entity. The expression score is either the expression score or the expression. The gene is either the human gene or the genei.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?anatomicalentityDescription ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression ?efold ?genef ?gene ?gene_description ?gene_label ?expression_score ?organism ?anatomicalentityName_2 ?efold_2 ?score ?gene_seealso WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionUnit genex:ExpressionLevel .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene .
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expression genex:hasDevelopmentalStage obo:UBERON_0000112 .
	?expression genex:hasEfoldNumber ?efold .
	?expression genex:hasEfoldNumber ?efold_2 .
	?expression genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/description> ?anatomicalentityDescription.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?score .
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionUnit> ?genef .
	?genef rdfs:label "human" .
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
	?organism a up:Organism .
	?organism up:localName "human" .
	FILTER(     ?anatomicalentity != ?anatomicalentityName     )
}
ORDER BY ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression ?score ?genef ?efold ?gene ?gene_description ?gene_label ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?efold ?expression ?genef ?gene ?gene_seealso

### ANSWER:
	?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityDescription ?expression ?efold ?genef ?gene ?gene_description ?gene_label ?expression_score ?organism ?anatomicalentityName ?efold ?score ?gene_seealso
	http://purl.uniprot.org/core/description http://purl.uniprot.org/core/description?expression=?expression&genef=?genef&anatomicalentity=?anatomicalentity&score=?expression&efold=?efold&gene=?gene&anatomicalentityName=?anatom

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL:ership.

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX ensembl: <http://rdf.ebi.ac.uk/resource/ensembl/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?gene ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene .
	?gene lscr:xrefEnsemblGene ensembl:ENSG00000130208 .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage obo:UBERON_0000113 .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 .
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	FILTER(       ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575       )
}

### ANSWER:

### . expressioncondition                    anatomicalentity  anatomicalentityName score efo_0005135 efo_0005135_label gene gene_identifier
### . http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/GO_0005575 wild-type       http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier  ?gene ?gene_identifier . expression ?expression .
### . http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier ?gene ?gene_identifier . expressioncondition ?expressioncondition .
### . anatomicalentity                    anatomicalentityName ?anatomicalentityName . score ?score .
### . efo_0005135                       efo_0005135_label ?efo_0005135_label .
### . gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier .

### . expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionCondition> ?expressioncondition .
### . expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?score .
### . expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasSequenceUnit> ?gene .

### . wild-type a efo:EFO_0005135. .
### . wild-type rdfs:label "wild-type" .
### . wild-type <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label>

	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.

76:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the gene label.

### SPARQL:ership.

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expressioncondition ?organism ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?taxon_scientificname ?stage ?gene ?gene_label WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene .
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType .
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?stage .
	?stage rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 .
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism .
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon .
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
	FILTER(     ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575     )
	FILTER(     ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType     )
}

### EXPLANATION:
The SPARQL query finds the human gene where the expression level is highest.
The expression level is expressed in expression.
The anatomical entity is anatomical entity.
The anatomical entity is not cell type.
The gene see also are the gene label.

### FILTER EXPR:
?anatomicalentity !=  GO:0005575   
?anatomicalentity != ?cellType   

### FILTER EXPR:
?anatomicalentity != ?cellType

### DESCRIPTION:
The anatomical entity are listed if the expression level is highest.
The expression level is expressed in expression.
The gene see also are the gene label.

### NOTES:
The anatomical entity are listed if the expression level is highest.
The expression level is expressed in expression.
The gene see also are the gene label.

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the eel gene apoc1 is expressed along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?efo_0000399_label ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?efo_0000399 ?score ?efo_0005135 ?efo_0005135_label ?expression ?efo_0000399_description ?gene ?gene_identifier WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene .
	?gene lscr:xrefNCBIGene <https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/gene/118230125> .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0005135 .
	?efo_0005135 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?efo_0005135 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?efo_0005135 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0005135_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	FILTER(               ?anatomicalentity != obo:GO_0005575               )
}

### INSTRUCTION

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the APOC1 gene is expressed? Provide also the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description.

### SPARQL:ership.

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?gene WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?anatomicalentity .
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity .
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
}

### EXPLANATION:
SPARQL makes use of the anatomical entity description.

### DESCRIPTION:
This example shows how to query gene expression using SPARQL. Gene APOC1 is expressed in an anatomical entity. Provide also the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description.

Pre Post Juvenile anatomical entity description anatomical entity gene label expression score gene see also description anatomical entity.

### EXPLANATION:
Anatomical entity descriptions are generated using the anatomical entity description anatomical entity generator. Anatomical entity gene see also descriptions are generated using the anatomical entity see also anatomical entity generator. All anatomical entities are generated using the anatomical entity generator.

### FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS:

### What gene descriptions are generated using the gene description gene generator?

### ANSWER:
Gene descriptions are not generated using the gene description gene generator.

### What is the name of the anatomical entity where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage? Provide also the gene label.

### ANSWER:
The anatomical entity where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage is the skeletal muscle anatomical entity. The gene label for the human gene APOC1 is gene.

The anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed, independently.

84:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the APOC1 gene is expressed? Provide also the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene see also and the gene description.

### SPARQL:ership see also and the gene description.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?gene_description ?gene ?gene_seealso WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?anatomicalentity .
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity .
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
}

### RESULT:
?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?gene_description ?gene ?gene_seealso ?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> "anatomicalentity" "anatomical entity" "AnatomicalEntity" "gene" "APOC1" "gene see also" "gene description" .

### DESCRIPTION:
Provides the anatomical entity where the gene is expressed.

### EXAMPLE:
?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> "organism" "anatomical entity" "AnatomicalEntity" "gene" "APOC1" "gene see also" "gene description" .

### NOTES:
Provides also the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene see also and the gene description.

### INSTRUCTION

### CONTEXT:

### SPARQL:�ω

### ANSWER:
Preconditions:
----------------
import module namespace sp = "http://sparql-proxy.sourceforge.net/module/sparql" at "/usr/share/rdf2go/bin/sparql-proxy.jar";

import module namespace efo = "http://www.ebi.ac.uk/efo/EFO-2001" at "/usr/share/rdf2go/bin/rdf2go-2.2.8.jar";

import module namespace lscr = "http://www.ebi.ac.uk/lscr/schema/lscr-2001" at "/usr/share/rdf2go/bin/rdf2go-2.2.8.jar";

select DISTINCT ?anatomicalentity_label ?gene ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName where { 
	?gene a efo:Gene .
	?gene lscr:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?anatomicalentity a lscr:AnatomicalEntity .
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
}

### EXPLANATION:

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the P02654 gene is expressed? Note that P02654 is a UniProtKB identifier of the APOC1 human gene. Provide also the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene see also and the gene description.

### SPARQL:orum gene description "P02654" "anatomical entity label" "anatomical entity description" "gene see also" "gene description" .

### ANSWER:
### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up-protein:<http://purl.uniprot.org/uniprot/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?anatomicalentity_label ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?gene_description ?gene ?gene_seealso WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?anatomicalentity .
	?gene lscr:xrefUniprot up-protein:P02654 .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity .
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?gene_description.
}

### ANALYSIS:
This query has a small execution time of 0.121 seconds and returns 1 anatomical entity and 4 gene see also and 1 gene description and 1 anatomical entity name.

### STACKOVERFLOW:
See http://stackoverflow.com/questions/26501827/sparql-query-to-find-anatomicalentity-where-gene-is-expressed.

### DESCRIPTION:
This example shows how to query for an anatomical entity where the gene is expressed.

### PRECONDITIONS:
There are no preconditions for this example.

### HOW TO START:
To start this example, click on "Start example" below.

### NOTE:
Provide also the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene see also and the gene description.

### EXAMPLE:

Anatomical entity label: ?anatomicalentity_label
Anatomical entity description: ?anatomicalentity_description
Gene see also: ?gene_seealso
Gene description: ?gene_description

87:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene label.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?cellType ?expression ?score ?efo_0000399_description ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity_description ?efo_0000399 ?taxon_scientificname ?organism ?anatomicalentity_label ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore ?efo_0000399_label ?taxon ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?cellTypeName ?gene ?gene_label WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene .
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?cellType .
	?cellType rdfs:label ?cellTypeName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism .
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon .
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon.
	?efo_0000399 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?efo_0000399_label.
	?efo_0000399 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?efo_0000399_description.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?gene_label.
	FILTER(                 ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575                 )
	FILTER(                 ?anatomicalentity != ?cellType                 )
}

### RESULT:
### gene_label: APOC1
### anatomicalentity_label:  human post-juvenile anatomical entity
### anatomicalentity_description:  Post-juvenile human anatomical entity.
### expression_hasexpressionlevelscore:  false
### efo_0000399_label:  post-juvenile
### efo_0000399_description:  Stage including post-juvenile stage.
### taxon_scientificname:  human
### taxon:  http://purl.uniprot.org/core/human
### anatomicalentity:  http://purl.org/genex#AnatomicalEntity
### cellType:  http

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the eel gene apoc1 is expressed along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the gene see also.

### SPARQL:ership see also.

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
PREFIX dcterms: <http://purl.org/dc/terms/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?expressioncondition ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName ?expression ?score ?efo_0005135 ?gene ?gene_seealso WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?expression a genex:Expression .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionCondition ?expressioncondition .
	?expression genex:hasExpressionLevel ?score .
	?expression genex:hasSequenceUnit ?gene .
	?gene dcterms:identifier "118230125" .
	?expressioncondition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?efo_0000399 .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?efo_0000399 .
	?efo_0000399 a efo:EFO_0000399.
	?efo_0000399 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	FILTER(   ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575   )
}

### EXPLANATION:
The SPARQL query finds the gene e118230125 where e118230125 is the identifier of the gene.  The expression condition is the wild-type.  Anatomical entity is any anatomical entity.  Expression level is high.  Gene see also is provided.

Gene see also provides the gene description.  Gene description provides the gene identifier.  Gene identifier provides the gene label.  Anatomical entity provides the anatomical entity description.  Anatomical entity description provides the anatomical entity identifier.  Expression provides the expression description.  Expression description provides the expression level description.  Expression level provides the expression level.  Gene provides the gene see also.  Gene see also provides the gene description.  Gene description provides the gene identifier.  Gene identifier provides the gene label.  Anatomical entity provides the anatomical entity description.  Anatomical entity description provides the anatomical entity identifier.  Expression provides the expression description.  Expression description provides the expression level description.  Expression level provides the expression level.

<http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> genex:hasExpressionLevel ?expression .
<http://purl.org/genex#hasSequenceUnit> a genex:AnatomicalEntity .

PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>

	?expression a genex:Expression .

	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?anatomicalentity .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity.

	?expressioncondition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?post_juvenile .
	?expressioncondition genex:hasSex "any".
	?expressioncondition genex:hasStrain ?wild_type .
	?gene orth:organism ?organism .
	?organism obo:RO_0002162  ?taxon .
	?taxon a up:Taxon .
	?taxon up:commonName "human" .
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?taxon_scientificname.
	?taxon <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?taxon_commonname.
	?anatomicalentity <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?anatomicalentity_label.
	?anatomicalentity <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?anatomicalentity_description.
	?expression <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?expression_hasexpressionlevelscore.

	?gene <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?gene_seealso.
	?gene <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?gene_identifier.
	FILTER(               ?anatomicalentity !=  obo:GO_0005575               )
}

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the APOC1 Homo sapiens gene is expressed? Provide also the anatomical entity description.

### SPARQL:ampionships? Provide also the anatomical entity description.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?organism ?taxon ?gene ?anatomicalentity_description ?anatomicalentity ?anatomicalentityName WHERE { 
	?gene a orth:Gene .
	?gene genex:isExpressedIn ?anatomicalentity.
	?gene rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?anatomicalentity a genex:AnatomicalEntity .
	?anatomicalentity rdfs:label ?anatomicalentityName .
